### ‚ùå Original (clunky, nominalization)

**Tyrosine phosphorylation by activated JAKs of cytokine-receptor cytoplasmic domains then provides binding sites for the Src-homology-2 domain of the STAT proteins.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®-‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° JAKs ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® STAT ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Src-homology-2 ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶π ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§*

üëâ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú (phosphorylation)** noun ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ Improved (clearer action)

**Activated JAKs phosphorylate the cytokine-receptor cytoplasmic domains, creating binding sites for the Src-homology-2 domain of STAT proteins.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° JAKs ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®-‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá STAT ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Src-homology-2 ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§*

üëâ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® **subject (JAKs)** ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá (**phosphorylate**)‡•§

### ‚úÖ More precise

**Activated JAKs phosphorylate tyrosine on cytokine-receptor cytoplasmic domains, which then provides binding sites for the Src-homology-2 domain of the STAT proteins.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° JAKs ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®-‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá STAT ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Src-homology-2 ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§*

---

### ‚úÖ Best Revised (actors + actions + clarity)

**Activated JAKs then phosphorylate tyrosine on cytokine-receptor cytoplasmic domains, providing binding sites for the STAT proteins' Src-homology-2 domain.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° JAKs ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®-‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç STAT ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Src-homology-2 ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§*

---

**Simplified alternative:**
**Activated JAKs phosphorylate the cytoplasmic domains of cytokine receptors, creating binding sites for the Src-homology-2 domain of STAT proteins.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° JAKs ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®-‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá STAT ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Src-homology-2 ‡¶°‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§*

---

üëâ Notice how the **subject (Activated JAKs)** is always close to the **verb (phosphorylate)** in the revised versions, making the sentence clearer and more powerful.

## 1.2

Exactly üëç You‚Äôve applied the **Actors and Actions** principles very well here. Let‚Äôs break it down with **English + Bangla** so you can clearly see how the revision improves clarity.

---

### ‚ùå Original (clunky, nominalization style)

**We subjected yeast to 20 min of amino acid deprivation and made ribosome-footprint and mRNA-abundance measurements.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ï‡ßá ‡ß®‡ß¶ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶¨‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶Æ-‡¶´‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ì mRNA-‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡•§*

üëâ Here, the action ‚Äúsubjected to deprivation‚Äù is unnecessarily complicated.

---

### ‚úÖ Improved (direct action)

**We deprived yeast of amino acids for 20 minutes and measured ribosome footprints and mRNA abundance.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡ß®‡ß¶ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡¶´‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ì mRNA ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§*

üëâ Now **subject = We**, **verbs = deprived, measured** ‚Üí clear and strong.

---

### ‚úÖ Revised with more clarity

**We deprived yeast of amino acids for 20 minutes and then measured ribosome footprints and mRNA abundance.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡ß®‡ß¶ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡¶´‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ì mRNA ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§*

üëâ Adding **‚Äúthen‚Äù** improves flow (first action ‚Üí second action).

---

‚ö° **Why this revision works better:**

* **Actors are clear:** ‚ÄúWe‚Äù is the doer.
* **Actions are strong verbs:** deprived, measured.
* **Order is logical:** first deprive, then measure.

## 1.3

Beautiful work üëå You‚Äôve applied the **Actors and Actions** rules to a very complex sentence and made it readable. Let‚Äôs refine this with **clear breakdown + Bangla translation** so you see why your revisions are stronger.

---

## ‚ùå Original (very clunky, nominalizations everywhere)

**The assumptions that all sites evolve at one of two evolutionary rates (conserved and nonconserved), that these rates are uniform across the genome, that sites evolve independently conditional on whether they are in conserved or nonconserved regions, and that the phylogenetic models for conserved and nonconserved regions have the same branch-length proportions, base compositions, and substitution patterns, all represent oversimplifications of the complex process of sequence evolution in eukaryotic genomes.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‚Äî‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡¶ú‡ßÅ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ, ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§, ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‚Äî‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ì‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£‡•§*

üëâ Hard to read because:

* Subject = *assumptions* is far from the verb *represent*.
* Long list is buried inside the subject.
* Action *oversimplify* is hidden in a noun *oversimplifications*.

---

## ‚úÖ Improved (clear actor + clear action)

**Researchers often assume that sites evolve at only two rates (conserved or nonconserved), that these rates are uniform across the genome, that sites evolve independently depending on their region, and that conserved and nonconserved regions share the same branch-length proportions, base compositions, and substitution patterns. These assumptions oversimplify the complex process of sequence evolution in eukaryotic genomes.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§, ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ì‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§*

üëâ Much clearer: subject = *researchers / assumptions*, verb = *assume / oversimplify*.

---

## ‚úÖ Revised (actor = assumptions)

**All these assumptions oversimplify the complex process of sequence evolution in eukaryotic genomes. These assumptions are that all sites evolve at one of two evolutionary rates (conserved and nonconserved), that these rates are uniform across the genome, that sites evolve independently based on their conservation status, and that the phylogenetic models for both regions share the same branch-length proportions, base compositions, and substitution patterns.**

**Bangla:**
*‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ì‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã: (‡ßß) ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, (‡ß®) ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®, (‡ß©) ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç (‡ß™) ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§, ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡•§*

üëâ Actor = *assumptions*
üëâ Action = *oversimplify*

---

## ‚úÖ Best Revised (actor = researchers, action = assume, oversimplify)

**We oversimplify the complex process of eukaryotic sequence evolution by assuming that:**

* sites evolve at one of two rates (conserved or nonconserved),
* these rates are uniform across the genome,
* sites evolve independently based on their region, and
* phylogenetic models for both regions share the same branch-length proportions, base compositions, and substitution patterns.

**Bangla:**
*‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ì‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‚Äî (‡ßß) ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§), (‡ß®) ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®, (‡ß©) ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç (‡ß™) ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§, ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡•§*

üëâ Very clear: subject = *we*, action = *oversimplify*, list = clean bullet points.

---

‚úÖ **Takeaway:**

* Original hides actions in nouns ‚Üí *oversimplifications*.
* Revisions make actions direct ‚Üí *assume, oversimplify*.
* Bullet structure helps readability in long technical writing.

### **Original**

> The number of different mechanisms that may exist for cells to interpret morphogens, and the importance of design features such as feedback or local cell-cell communication, is unclear.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶°‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑-‡¶ü‡ßÅ-‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Verb: *is unclear* ‚Üí ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶≤, ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÄ‡¶®‡•§

### **First Revised**

> It is unclear how many different mechanisms cells use to interpret morphogens, or how important design features such as feedback or local cell-cell communication are.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶°‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑-‡¶ü‡ßÅ-‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£, ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Subject: *It* ‚Üí dummy subject, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§
* Actors: *cells, design features* ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* Verbs: *use, are* ‚Üí ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡•§

### **Second Revised (Clearer)**

> How cells interpret morphogens and how design features like feedback or local communication influence this process remain unclear.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶°‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Subject: *How cells interpret... and how design features... influence...* ‚Üí ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ actors ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
* Actors: *cells, design features* ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* Verbs: *interpret, influence, remain unclear* ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ì ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡•§
* Flow: ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶£‡•§

---

‚úÖ **‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø:**

* ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤ subject (*cells*, *design features*) ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
* ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ action verbs ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§
* ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡•§

---

üëâ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ **exercise set** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ nominalized ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (‡¶á‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶ø), ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ actor‚Äìverb ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá? ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Would you like me to make that worksheet?

### **Original Sentence**

> Furthermore, the application of new technologies to further understand the biology of the adipocyte, including location analysis, global DNase hypersensitivity, high-throughput RNA-interference screens and computational strategies, promises to enhance our knowledge of this once-neglected cell.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶¨‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ó‚Äî‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏, ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≤ DNase ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø, ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á-‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü RNA-‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßå‡¶∂‡¶≤‚Äî‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏, ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≤ DNase ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø, ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á-‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü RNA-‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßå‡¶∂‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶¨‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Actor: *new technologies* ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø subject ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* Verbs: *will help, understand, enhance* ‚Üí ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ action verbs‡•§
* Flow: ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

### **Revised 2**

> Furthermore, new technologies‚Äîsuch as location analysis, global DNase hypersensitivity, high-throughput RNA-interference screens, and computational strategies‚Äîpromise to enhance our knowledge of the once-neglected adipocyte by helping us understand its biology.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏, ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≤ DNase ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø, ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á-‡¶•‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü RNA-‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßå‡¶∂‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶¨‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∑ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Subject: *technologies* ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® verb *promise*-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡•§
* Actor‚Äìverb ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü (*technologies promise, us understand*)‡•§
* ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§

### **Revised 3 (Most Compact)**

> New technologies‚Äîsuch as location analysis, DNase hypersensitivity mapping, RNA-interference screens, and computational strategies‚Äîpromise to deepen our understanding of adipocyte biology.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏, DNase ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶Ç, RNA-‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßå‡¶∂‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶¨‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶≠‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Subject: *new technologies* ‚Üí ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ actor‡•§
* Verb: *promise to deepen* ‚Üí ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ action‡•§
* ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‚Üí ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡•§

---

‚úÖ **‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã (Bangla):**

* *technologies* ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø actor ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* Nominalization ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá (*the application of technologies* ‚Üí *technologies*)‡•§

* ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ (Revised 3) ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡•§

üëâ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ **‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø (original nominalized + ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá actor‚Äìverb ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, ‡¶∏‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßÅ)‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ mini worksheet ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶á?

‚úÖ **‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã (Bangla):**

‚úÖ **‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã (Bangla):**

* ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

üëâ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡ß´‚Äì‡ß¨‡¶ü‡¶æ **original (passive/nominalized) scientific sentences** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø actor‚Äìverb ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® (‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ clue + model answer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶¨)?

### **Original Sentence**

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶ï‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ K-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç T-‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ì‡¶∏‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶á‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Subject: *A number of promoters* ‚Üí ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ actor-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶®‡•§
* Verb: *exhibited* ‚Üí ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡ßü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡•§

### **Revised 1**

> A number of promoters showed significant positive correlations between the footprinting estimated distribution of K and the nucleosome score from T-cells.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶ï‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ K-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç T-‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ì‡¶∏‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶á‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

* Verb: *showed* ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ì ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡•§

### **Revised 2**

> For a number of promoters, the distribution of K estimated from footprinting correlated positively with the nucleosome score estimated from T-cells.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶ï‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶´‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ K-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶£ T-‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ì‡¶∏‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Actor: *the distribution of K* ‚Üí ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤ data ‡¶ï‡ßá subject ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* Verb: *correlated* ‚Üí ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
* Passive ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‚Üí active voice‡•§

### **Revised 3 (Most Compact)**

> Several promoters showed strong positive correlations between footprinting-based K distributions and nucleosome scores from T-cells.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶ï‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç-‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï K-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç T-‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ì‡¶∏‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶á‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Subject: *promoters* ‚Üí actor ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§
* Verb: *showed* ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
* Phrase: *footprinting-based K distributions* ‚Üí ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§‡•§

---

‚úÖ **‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã (Bangla):**

* Actor (*promoters* ‡¶¨‡¶æ *distribution*) ‡¶ï‡ßá subject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* Action verb (*showed, correlated*) ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* Revised 2 data-‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï, Revised 3 ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá compact ‡¶ì natural‡•§

---

üëâ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ **original passive/nominalized biology sentences** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã), ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø actor‚Äìverb ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßá rewrite ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá **Bangla translation + feedback** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶¨‡•§
‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡ß´‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á?

### **Original Sentence**

> In this study, we subjected seven different primate species to comparative analysis of the radial distribution pattern of human chromosome 18- and 19-homologous chromatin by three-dimensional fluorescence in situ hybridization.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®-‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡ßß‡ßÆ ‡¶ì ‡ßß‡ßØ-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Subject: *we* ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‚Üí verb: *subjected‚Ä¶ to analysis* (nominalized, ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶®)‡•§
* Action (‚Äúanalyze‚Äù) noun ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá (*analysis*)‡•§
* ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡•§

---

### **Revised 1**

> In this study, we used three-dimensional fluorescence in situ hybridization to compare the radial distribution pattern of human chromosome 18- and 19-homologous chromatin in seven different primate species.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®-‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡ßß‡ßÆ ‡¶ì ‡ßß‡ßØ-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Actor: *we* ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø subject‡•§
* Verbs: *used, compare* ‚Üí ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ action verbs‡•§
* Nominalization ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§

### **Revised 2**

> In this study, we compared seven primate species, using three-dimensional fluorescence in situ hybridization to analyze the radial distribution pattern of their chromatin homologous to human chromosomes 18 and 19.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®-‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡ßß‡ßÆ ‡¶ì ‡ßß‡ßØ-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Actor: *we* ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§
* Verbs: *compared, analyze* ‚Üí ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£ action, ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
* Flow: ‡¶Ø‡ßå‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡•§

### **Revised 3 (Most Compact)**

> In this study, we used three-dimensional fluorescence in situ hybridization to compare the radial distribution of chromosome 18- and 19-homologous chromatin across seven primate species.

**‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶:**
‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®-‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡ßß‡ßÆ ‡¶ì ‡ßß‡ßØ-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

üîé ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£:

* Subject: *we* ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü actor‡•§
* Verbs: *used, compare* ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú, ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡•§
* Compact ‚Üí ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶£ ‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§

---

‚úÖ **‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã (Bangla):**

* *subjected‚Ä¶ to analysis* (‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶≤ nominalization) ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* Actor (*we*) ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ verbs (*used, compare, analyze*) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§
* Revised 3 ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

---

üëâ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® **nominalized scientific sentences** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø actor‚Äìverb ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá rewrite ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ translation + feedback ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶¨‡•§
‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á ‡ß´‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® practice sentence ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á?






# 2

Here‚Äôs a concise **summary of the lecture on Cohesion, Coherence, and Emphasis in Scientific Writing** (Dr. Khondaker A. Mamun):

---

### **Principle 1: Put New Information Last (Cohesion)**

* Begin sentences with **familiar (old) information** ‚Üí provides context and links to prior ideas.
* End sentences with **new (unfamiliar) information** ‚Üí emphasizes what‚Äôs important.
* This makes writing **clear, cohesive, and easy to follow**.
* **Revision technique**: underline new info in each sentence, ensure it comes last.

---

### **Principle 2: Use Passive Voice Judiciously**

* **Active voice**: clearer, livelier, shows responsibility (e.g., ‚ÄúWe proved the theorem‚Äù).
* **Passive voice**: acceptable, but risky if overused. Common issues:

  * **Ambiguity**: actor is hidden (who did the work?).
  * **Dangling modifiers**: mismatch between implied and real subject.
  * **Wordiness**: longer, weaker writing.
* **When useful**: to emphasize results or maintain old‚Üínew information flow.
* **Tip**: Avoid the myth that science must avoid first-person pronouns‚Äîauthors should take responsibility.

---

### **Principle 3: Ensure Coherence (First & Last Sentences Match)**

* A **paragraph = one main thought**.
* First sentence introduces topic, last sentence should reinforce it.
* If the paragraph starts on one subject but drifts to another, coherence is lost.
* **Revision technique**: Check if first and last sentences align; make sure all middle sentences support the central idea.

---

### **General Advice**

* Scientific writing should be **clear, concise, and logically structured**.
* Use **cohesion** (sentences linked), **coherence** (paragraph unity), and **emphasis** (important info at the end).
* Balance **active vs. passive voice** to avoid ambiguity while maintaining flow.
* Keep writing short, precise, and free from confusion.

---

Would you like me to also create a **one-page quick-reference guide (with examples)** that you can use while writing?



Great! Let‚Äôs carefully **revise each sentence** using the three principles:

1. **Put new information last** (so sentences flow old ‚Üí new).
2. **Use passive voice judiciously** (prefer active when actor is clear).
3. **Match first & last sentence of paragraphs** (stay coherent).

---

### **Revisions**

**1. Original:**
These data were then subjected to hierarchical clustering using the Pearson correlation as the distance metric.

---

**Original:**
These data were then subjected to hierarchical clustering using the Pearson correlation as the distance metric.

**Revised:**
We applied hierarchical clustering to these data, using the Pearson correlation as the distance metric.

---

### **Why this revision works (English explanation):**

1. **Active vs Passive:**

   * Original uses passive voice: *‚Äúwere subjected‚Äù*.
   * Revised uses active voice with a clear actor: *‚ÄúWe applied‚Ä¶‚Äù*. This makes the sentence direct and easier to read.

2. **Clarity of Actor:**

   * In science, hiding the actor (*who did the analysis*) often makes sentences ambiguous. The revision states clearly: *‚ÄúWe applied‚Ä¶‚Äù*.

3. **Cohesion (old ‚Üí new):**

   * The sentence starts with old information (*‚Äúthese data‚Äù*).
   * It ends with new information (*‚ÄúPearson correlation as the distance metric‚Äù*).
   * This order ensures logical flow and emphasis on what matters most.

---

### **‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ (Bangla Explanation):**

**‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Original):**
‚ÄúThese data were then subjected‚Ä¶‚Äù ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø passive voice ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶ï‡ßá data-‡¶ï‡ßá clustering ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡•§

**‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßã‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Revised):**
‚ÄúWe applied hierarchical clustering‚Ä¶‚Äù ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá active voice ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ Actor (‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ = researchers) ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

**‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã:**

1. **Passive ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Active:** ‚Äúsubjected‚Äù ‡¶ï‡ßá active ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Äúwe applied‡•§‚Äù ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶® ‚Üí ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø:** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Äúthese data‚Äù (‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‚ÄúPearson correlation‚Äù (‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ flow ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**

---

üëâ ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶ø + ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã worksheet ‡¶ü‡¶æ **‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡ßü (English + Bangla)** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶¨, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã exercise ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á?

**2. Original:**
We designated the putative GRB target genes as the human TFs that were under a HCNE density peak and whose orthologs were in conserved synteny with an array of HCNEs in human\:zebrafish alignments. Density peaks and syntenic regions were downloaded from the Ancora Genome Browser.


*(Active voice, new info ‚Äúhuman\:zebrafish alignments‚Äù and ‚ÄúAncora Genome Browser‚Äù placed at the end for emphasis.)*


**Original (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ GRB-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨ TFs ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã HCNE density peak-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ orthologs ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨:‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶∂ alignment-‡¶è HCNE-‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø array-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá conserved synteny-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§ Density peaks ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç syntenic regions Ancora Genome Browser ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§

**Revised (English):**
We designated as putative GRB target genes the human TFs located under an HCNE density peak and whose orthologs were in conserved synteny with arrays of HCNEs in human\:zebrafish alignments. We downloaded density peaks and syntenic regions from the Ancora Genome Browser.

**Revised (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ GRB-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨ TFs-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HCNE density peak-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ orthologs ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨:‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶∂ alignment-‡¶è HCNEs-‡¶è‡¶∞ arrays-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá conserved synteny-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Ancora Genome Browser ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá density peaks ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç syntenic regions ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§

---

### **Why this revision works (English Explanation):**

1. **Active vs Passive:** Actor (‚ÄúWe‚Äù) is explicit in both sentences, avoiding ambiguity.
2. **Old ‚Üí New (Cohesion):**

   * Starts with old info (*GRB target genes*).
   * Ends with new info (*human\:zebrafish alignments*, *Ancora Genome Browser*).
3. **Clarity:** Sentence structure is smoother and less overloaded.
4. **Emphasis:** New concepts are placed at the end for natural emphasis.

---

### **‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:**

* **‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Original):** ‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡•§ Actor ‚Äú‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‚Äù ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
* **‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßã‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Revised):**

  * Actor ‚Äú‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‚Äù ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§
  * ‚ÄúGRB-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‚Äù ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‚Äúhuman\:zebrafish alignment‚Äù ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‚ÄúAncora Genome Browser‚Äù ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ï‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* **‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤:** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

üëâ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® **Exercise 1 + 2 ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá bilingual (English + ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ full conversions)** ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø 3‚Äì6 ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® **Exercise 1 ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ 2 ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá bilingual format** ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á?

---

**3. Original:**
By analyzing all of the available mouse cDNA sequences, it was found that the mouse genome encodes at least 44,000 distinct transcriptional units; a transcriptional unit comprises all the RNAs that share a common exonic sequence transcribed from the same genomic strand.

### **Original (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**

‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶∏ cDNA ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶∏ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ ‡ß™‡ß™,‡ß¶‡ß¶‡ß¶‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶§‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá; ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ RNA ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Revised (English):**

By analyzing all available mouse cDNA sequences, we found that the mouse genome encodes at least 44,000 distinct transcriptional units. A transcriptional unit includes all RNAs that share a common exonic sequence transcribed from the same genomic strand.

### **Revised (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**

‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶∏ cDNA ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶∏ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ ‡ß™‡ß™,‡ß¶‡ß¶‡ß¶‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶§‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ RNA, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Why this revision works (English Explanation):**

1. **Avoids ambiguous actor:** Original used *‚Äúit was found‚Äù* (unclear who found it). Revision uses *‚Äúwe found‚Äù* (clear actor).
2. **Old ‚Üí New (Cohesion):**

   * Starts with familiar info (*mouse cDNA sequences*).
   * Ends with important new info (*44,000 transcriptional units*).
3. **Clarity:** The long sentence is split into two. The definition of transcriptional unit is separated, so the reader processes it more easily.
4. **Emphasis:** The key result (*44,000 units*) is highlighted at the end of the first sentence.

---

### **‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:**

* **‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Original):** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá actor ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá *‚Äúit was found‚Äù* ‚Üí ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶®‡•§
* **‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßã‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Revised):**

  * Actor ‚Äú‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‚Äù ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‚ÄúcDNA sequences‚Äù (‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø) ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá, ‚Äú44,000 distinct transcriptional units‚Äù (‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø) ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá definition ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* **‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤:** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

*(Avoids ambiguous actor ‚Äúit was found,‚Äù keeps clarity.)*

---

**4. Original:**
Improvements are expected in the predictive power of all the scores being computed on multispecies alignments.

### **Original (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**

‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÅ-‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞ alignment-‡¶è ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∂‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Revised (English):**

Our method will improve the predictive power of all scores computed on multispecies alignments.

### **Revised (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÅ-‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞ alignment-‡¶è ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Why this revision works (English Explanation):**

1. **Active vs Passive:**

   * Original: *‚ÄúImprovements are expected‚Äù* (passive, vague‚Äîwho expects?).
   * Revised: *‚ÄúOur method will improve‚Äù* (active, clear actor, direct).

2. **Old ‚Üí New (Cohesion):**

   * Old info: *‚Äúour method‚Äù* (the subject of the study).
   * New info: *‚Äúmultispecies alignments‚Äù* (technical detail), placed at the end for emphasis.

3. **Clarity and Conciseness:**

   * Original had two passive-like verbs (*‚Äúare expected, being computed‚Äù*), making it wordy.
   * Revised uses a direct verb (*‚Äúwill improve‚Äù*), making it shorter and stronger.

---

### **‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:**

* **‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Original):** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá actor ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá *‚Äú‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∂‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‚Äù* ‚Üí ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∂‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø passive ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶∂‡ßã‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
* **‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßã‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Revised):**

  * Actor ‚Äú‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‚Äù ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø (‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú/‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø) ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‚Äúmultispecies alignment‚Äù ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* **‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤:** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø active, ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

---

üëâ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø **Exercise 1‚Äì4** ‡¶è‡¶∞ bilingual ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§
‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø **Exercise 5 ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 6**-‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá bilingual (Original + Revised + Explanation) ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã worksheet ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá?


---

**5. Original:**
With the development of molecular embryology and the coming of the post-genomic era, the molecular mechanisms of morphological evolution have recently begun to be elucidated.
### **Original (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**

‡¶Æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü-‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶£‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Revised (English):**

With the development of molecular embryology and the post-genomic era, researchers have recently begun to elucidate the molecular mechanisms of morphological evolution.

### **Revised (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**

‡¶Æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü-‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá, ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶£‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

---

### **Why this revision works (English Explanation):**

1. **Active vs Passive:**

   * Original: *‚Äúhave recently begun to be elucidated‚Äù* ‚Üí passive, vague, and wordy.
   * Revised: *‚Äúresearchers have recently begun to elucidate‚Äù* ‚Üí active, clear actor, shorter, and direct.

2. **Clarity:**

   * Passive made it sound like the processes ‚Äúexplained themselves.‚Äù
   * Revision assigns responsibility to *researchers*, which is accurate and easy to follow.

3. **Cohesion (Old ‚Üí New):**

   * Old info: *molecular embryology, post-genomic era*.
   * New info: *molecular mechanisms of morphological evolution*.
   * New info is placed at the end for emphasis.

---

### **‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:**

* **‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Original):** ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá *‚Äú‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‚Äù*, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ passive‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∂‡ßã‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* **‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßã‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Revised):**

  * Actor ‚Äú‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‚Äù ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø active voice ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø (‡¶Æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶ú‡¶ø + ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü-‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ó) ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø (‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶£‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶æ) ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* **‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤:** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü, ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡•§

---

üëâ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ **Exercise 6** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ì bilingual (Original + Revised + Explanation) ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã worksheet ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á?

---

**6. Original:**
‡¶ö‡¶Æ‡ßé‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ üëç ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶ü‡¶æ, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé **Exercise 6**, bilingual ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

---

### **Original (English):**

To assess the degree of enrichment of enhancer activities in predicted tissues, we compared the relative frequency of enhancers for each of the three tissues examined here with a background set of 528 previously tested sequences predicted to be developmental enhancers on the basis of extreme sequence constraint that were not associated with a prior tissue specificity prediction.

### **Original (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**

‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡ß´‡ß®‡ßÆ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ-‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

---

### **Revised (English):**

To assess the enrichment of enhancer activities in predicted tissues, we compared the frequency of enhancers in each of the three examined tissues with a background set of 528 previously tested sequences. These sequences had been predicted as developmental enhancers based on extreme sequence constraint but were not associated with any prior tissue-specificity prediction.

### **Revised (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ):**

‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡ß´‡ß®‡ßÆ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ-‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

---

### **Why this revision works (English Explanation):**

1. **Sentence length reduced:**

   * Original: one very long, complex sentence (hard to read).
   * Revised: split into two shorter sentences ‚Üí much easier to follow.

2. **Clarity of structure:**

   * First sentence: describes the **comparison** (main action).
   * Second sentence: explains the **background set**.
   * Readers process info step by step.

3. **Cohesion (Old ‚Üí New):**

   * Old info: *predicted tissues, enhancers*.
   * New info: *tissue-specificity prediction* at the end.

4. **Active voice retained:**

   * Actor *‚Äúwe compared‚Äù* is explicit and clear.

---

### **‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:**

* **‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Original):** ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¢‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
* **‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßã‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Revised):**

  * ‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
  * ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú (‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ) ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
  * ‚Äútissue-specificity prediction‚Äù ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
* **‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤:** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

---

‚úÖ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá **Exercise 1‚Äì6 bilingual (Original + Revised + Explanation)** ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ bilingual worksheet (PDF ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã)** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®?


*(Breaks up the long, heavy sentence for clarity; puts new info last; keeps coherence.)*

---

‚úÖ Each revision:

* Flows **old ‚Üí new information**
* Uses **active voice when possible**
* Keeps **clear subject-verb-object structure**
* Improves **clarity and emphasis**

---

Would you like me to **format this into a neat worksheet with "Original ‚Üí Revised" pairs side by side**, so you can use it directly for study or teaching?



# 3

Here‚Äôs a **clear and compact summary** of the material on **Concision and Simplicity in Scientific Writing**:

---

## üîë Principles

1. **Omit needless words**

   * Remove filler phrases (e.g., *note that, it should be noted that, so-called*).
   * Replace wordy phrases with single words (e.g., *due to the fact that ‚Üí because*).
   * Cut redundancy (*‚Äúnew invention‚Äù ‚Üí ‚Äúinvention‚Äù*).
   * Avoid excessive hedging (*may possibly suggest ‚Üí suggests*).

2. **Prefer simple words**

   * Use short, direct words instead of inflated ones.

     * *methodology ‚Üí method*
     * *utilize ‚Üí use*
     * *deleterious ‚Üí harmful*
   * Long words don‚Äôt make writing impressive‚Äîjust harder to read.

3. **Use simple subjects**

   * Don‚Äôt cram too many details into the subject of a sentence.
   * Keep subject (actor) close to verb (action).
   * Break long, complex sentences into smaller ones.

4. **Use adjectives/adverbs frugally**

   * Avoid meaningless intensifiers (*very, extremely*).
   * Avoid repetition (*completely and utterly alone ‚Üí alone*).
   * Limit hedging (*may possibly identify ‚Üí identifies*).
   * Don‚Äôt insult readers with words like *obviously, clearly*.
   * Don‚Äôt oversell your work (*groundbreaking, exciting new*).

---

## ‚úçÔ∏è Revision Techniques

* Search for filler phrases and cut them.
* Replace complex words with simple ones.
* Simplify long subjects, split into multiple sentences.
* Highlight modifiers (adjectives/adverbs) ‚Üí keep only those that add meaning.

---

## ‚úÖ Example Improvements

* *Different kinds of methodology ‚Üí different methods*
* *We are planning to consider possible options ‚Üí We are considering how to extend our results*
* *Epigenetic events contribute to the etiology of diabetes ‚Üí Epigenetic problems can cause diabetes*

---

üëâ **Core Idea**:
Good scientific writing is **clear, concise, and simple**. Remove clutter, prefer short words, keep sentences direct, and use modifiers sparingly.

---

Would you like me to make you a **one-page cheat sheet** (with a table of common wordy ‚Üí simple replacements) so you can use it quickly while writing?







## 3.1

Got it üëç Let‚Äôs analyze and revise your sentence step by step, following the **concision and simplicity principles**:

---

### **Original Sentence**

> *Most used CTSSs in the PMA time-course are observed to be, on average, approximately 450 bp away from an H3K9 AC island.*

**Bangla Meaning:**
PMA ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ-‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ CTSS ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ó‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡ß™‡ß´‡ß¶ bp ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø H3K9 AC ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßÄ‡¶™ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Problems in Original**

1. **Passive voice**: ‚Äúare observed to be‚Äù ‚Üí weaker and wordier.
2. **Redundant hedging**: ‚Äúon average‚Äù + ‚Äúapproximately‚Äù ‚Üí both imply estimation, so one is enough.
3. **Overstuffed subject**: ‚ÄúMost used CTSSs in the PMA time-course‚Äù ‚Üí heavy and clunky.

---

### **Revised Versions**

**Option 1 (Concise, Direct):**
‚úî *In the PMA time-course, the most used CTSSs are about 450 bp from an H3K9 AC island.*

**Bangla:**
PMA ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ-‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ CTSS ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡ß™‡ß´‡ß¶ bp ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø H3K9 AC ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßÄ‡¶™ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

**Option 2 (More Active Voice):**
‚úî *In the PMA time-course, we found that the most used CTSSs lie about 450 bp from an H3K9 AC island.*

**Bangla:**
PMA ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ-‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ CTSS ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡ß™‡ß´‡ß¶ bp ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø H3K9 AC ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßÄ‡¶™ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### **What We Fixed**

* Simplified subject ‚Üí moved ‚Äúin the PMA time-course‚Äù to the front.
* Removed redundancy ‚Üí kept only *about*.
* Replaced weak phrase ‚Äúare observed to be‚Äù with either **active voice (we found)** or **direct verb (lie, are)**.

---

üëâ Do you want me to keep making **two revised versions (concise vs active)** for each of your sentences so you can pick the style that fits your paper best?

---

### **What We Fixed**

* Removed unnecessary repetition of ‚Äúcomplex‚Äù.
* Simplified structure ‚Üí short and readable.
* Gave two styles:

  * **Option 1** = strong, concise, active voice.
  * **Option 2** = still formal, keeps the ‚Äúone of the complexes‚Äù nuance.

üëâ Do you want me to **always provide both a concise version and a formal-but-simple version** for your sentences, so you can choose depending on your paper‚Äôs tone?



## 3.3

---

### **Original Sentence**

> *The mechanistic connections among levels of phenotypic variation, for example, between spatial or temporal patterns of gene expression and morphology, determine how development constrains or channels evolution.*

**Bangla Meaning:**
‡¶´‡ßá‡¶®‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó, ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Problems in Original**

1. **Long, overloaded subject:** ‚ÄúThe mechanistic connections among levels of phenotypic variation‚Ä¶‚Äù ‚Üí heavy and hard to parse.
2. **Nested example in the middle:** interrupts flow.
3. **Abstract wording:** ‚Äúdetermine how development constrains or channels evolution‚Äù could be simpler.

---

### **Revised Versions**

**Option 1 (Concise, Direct):**
‚úî *Connections between gene expression patterns and morphology show how development shapes evolution.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

**Option 2 (Formal but Simple):**
‚úî *Mechanistic links between phenotypic variation‚Äîsuch as spatial or temporal gene expression and morphology‚Äîreveal how development constrains evolution.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶´‡ßá‡¶®‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‚Äî‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶ú‡¶ø‚Äî‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **What We Fixed**

* **Simplified subject:** moved example (‚Äúgene expression and morphology‚Äù) into parentheses/dashes or direct form.
* **Cut redundancy:** ‚Äúdetermine how development constrains or channels‚Äù ‚Üí simplified to *shapes* or *constrains*.
* **Flow improved:** shorter, smoother phrasing.

---

üëâ Do you want me to **prioritize concise clarity (Option 1)** or **retain some formal academic tone (Option 2)** when rewriting your sentences?



## 3.4
Perfect ‚Äî let‚Äôs refine this one using **concision and simplicity rules**.

---

### **Original Sentence**

> *The scrutiny by natural selection is held to be greater for exons than their flanking intron sequences due to the explicit encoding of molecular function by exons.*

**Bangla Meaning:**
‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ú‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶£‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Problems in Original**

1. **Wordy subject:** ‚ÄúThe scrutiny by natural selection is held to be‚Ä¶‚Äù ‚Üí clunky.
2. **Redundancy:** ‚Äúdue to the explicit encoding of molecular function by exons‚Äù ‚Üí can be simplified.
3. **Passive/hedging:** ‚Äúis held to be‚Äù ‚Üí weak, indirect.

---

### **Revised Versions**

**Option 1 (Concise, Direct):**
‚úî *Natural selection acts more strongly on exons than on their flanking introns because exons encode molecular functions.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶£‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

**Option 2 (Formal but Simple):**
‚úî *Exons face stronger natural selection than flanking introns, since they directly encode molecular functions.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶® ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶ñ‡ßÄ‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶£‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **What We Fixed**

* Replaced **‚Äúscrutiny by natural selection is held to be greater‚Äù** ‚Üí ‚Äúnatural selection acts more strongly‚Äù / ‚Äúexons face stronger selection.‚Äù
* Simplified **‚Äúdue to the explicit encoding of molecular function by exons‚Äù** ‚Üí ‚Äúbecause exons encode molecular functions.‚Äù
* Shifted to **active, direct phrasing**.

---

üëâ Do you want me to also provide a **super-compressed version** (one-liner with minimum words) for each sentence, in case you need *ultra-concise* text for figures, captions, or slides?



## 3.5
Nice example üëç Let‚Äôs apply the concision and simplicity principles.

---

### **Original Sentence**

> *A phylogenetic tree based on the number of differentially expressed genes between species recapitulates their known phylogeny.*

**Bangla Meaning:**
‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Problems in Original**

1. **Wordy subject:** ‚ÄúA phylogenetic tree based on the number of differentially expressed genes between species‚Äù ‚Üí too heavy.
2. **Verb choice:** ‚Äúrecapitulates‚Äù is a fancy word; ‚Äúmatches‚Äù or ‚Äúreflects‚Äù is simpler.
3. **Clarity:** ‚Äúbetween species‚Äù could be positioned better for readability.

---

### **Revised Versions**

**Option 1 (Concise, Direct):**
‚úî *A phylogenetic tree from differentially expressed gene counts matches the known phylogeny.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

**Option 2 (Formal but Simple):**
‚úî *Phylogenetic trees built from species differences in gene expression reflect their known evolutionary relationships.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **What We Fixed**

* Broke down the heavy subject into a lighter form.
* Replaced **‚Äúrecapitulates‚Äù** ‚Üí ‚Äúmatches‚Äù / ‚Äúreflects‚Äù (clearer, simpler).
* Adjusted word order for smoother flow.

---

## 3.6

Let‚Äôs simplify this one carefully üëå.

---

### **Original Sentence**

**Bangla Meaning:**
‡¶™‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá (‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ø-‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá), ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶á svb-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

---

### **Problems in Original**

1. **Heavy subject:** ‚ÄúModifications of the trichome pattern that have been examined in insects‚Ä¶‚Äù ‚Üí long and clunky.
2. **Redundancy:** ‚Äúare so far all attributable‚Äù ‚Üí can be reduced to ‚Äúso far all come from‚Äù / ‚Äúso far all due to.‚Äù
3. **Parentheses interrupt flow** ‚Üí better to integrate smoothly.

‚úî *In insects, all examined trichome pattern changes‚Äîwhether from lab mutations or evolutionary diversification‚Äîso far stem from altered svb expression.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶™‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá, ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‚Äî‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‚Äî‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ svb ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÇ‡¶§‡•§

---

**Option 2 (Formal but Simple):**
‚úî *So far, insect trichome pattern modifications studied in the lab or through evolutionary diversification have all been linked to changes in svb expression.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§, ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® svb ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### **What We Fixed**

* Moved ‚Äúin insects‚Äù to the front ‚Üí cleaner subject.
* Replaced ‚Äúare so far all attributable to‚Äù ‚Üí ‚Äústem from‚Äù / ‚Äúlinked to.‚Äù

## 3.7

**Bangla Meaning:**
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶£‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á‡•§

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶á, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

## 3.8

Great sentence ‚Äî let‚Äôs polish it using the concision and simplicity principles.

---

### **Original Sentence**

> *These sequences are generally among the least constrained in the genome, so they constitute a plausible neutral standard accounting for regional variation in mutation and recombination rates.*

**Bangla Meaning:**
‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¶‡¶£‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### **Problems in Original**

1. **Wordy phrase:** ‚Äúconstitute a plausible neutral standard accounting for‚Äù ‚Üí heavy and abstract.
2. **Two layers of hedging:** ‚Äúgenerally‚Äù + ‚Äúplausible.‚Äù
3. **Long subject‚Äìpredicate structure:** hard to parse smoothly.

---

### **Revised Versions**

**Option 1 (Concise, Direct):**
‚úî *These sequences are among the least constrained in the genome and provide a neutral standard for regional variation in mutation and recombination rates.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¶‡¶£‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

**Option 2 (Formal but Simple):**
‚úî *Because these sequences are among the least constrained in the genome, they serve as a neutral reference for regional variation in mutation and recombination rates.*

**Bangla:**
‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

**Option 3 (Ultra Concise, figure-caption style):**
‚úî *Least-constrained sequences serve as neutral references for mutation and recombination variation.*

**Bangla:**
